BB-001-010 [a] the voc. particle; precedes a noun in the voc. case, beginning with an asp.con.; and suffers elision before vow.
BB-001-020 [a] his; poss.pron. precedes asp.con.; and suffers elision before vow.
BB-001-030 [a] her; poss.pron. precedes unasp.con.; and takes h- before vow.
BB-001-040 [a] for : do; fulfils the function of `that' in relative clauses; and precedes asp.con. of verb
BB-001-050 [a] for : do; fulfils the function of `to' before infinitives; and precedes asp.con. of verb-noun
BB-001-060 [a] for : do, de = to, off, in prepositional phrases; and precedes asp.con.
BB-001-070 [a] for : an = in and from in prep.phr.; and precedes unasp.con.
BB-001-080 [a'] the; art. precedes asp.con. of noun
BB-001-090 [a'] for : ag = at, engaged in; precedes unasp.con. of verb-noun
